However, in reality, perfume essential oils and synthetic perfumes are entirely different and have their own characteristics.\n\n4.Alcohol Content A fundamental difference between these two lies in the alcohol content. Alcohol is considered a crucial element in creating the fragrance variations in synthetic perfumes, with alcohol making up as much as 50% to 70% of a perfume bottle. In contrast, perfume essential oils contain very little or even no alcohol. Instead, oils like Jojoba or grapeseed oil are often used to create various scents in essential oils.
